  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_3155b7e1-3005-446d-9553-63101029e026'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<span id="freeTextContainer9370065814864257951">In the future, the world is at war. <br/><br/>For the last decade, King Lazuli of the Eastern Empire has systematically taken over the world. No one knows much about him other than a series of impossible facts: he cannot die, he has not aged since the conflict began, and he wants to rule the world.<br/><br/>All Serenity Freeman has known is bloodshed. War has taken away her mother, her home, </span>
  <span id="freeText9370065814864257951" style="display:none">In the future, the world is at war. <br /><br />For the last decade, King Lazuli of the Eastern Empire has systematically taken over the world. No one knows much about him other than a series of impossible facts: he cannot die, he has not aged since the conflict began, and he wants to rule the world.<br /><br />All Serenity Freeman has known is bloodshed. War has taken away her mother, her home, her safety. As the future emissary of the Western United Nations, the last autonomous region of the globe, she is responsible for forging alliances where she can. <br /><br />Surrender is on the horizon. The king can taste it; Serenity feels it deep within her bones. There is no other option. Now the two must come face to face. For Serenity, that means confronting the man who’s taken everything from her. For the king, it means meeting the one woman he can’t conquer. But when they meet, something happens. Cruelty finds redemption. <br /><br />Only in war, everything comes with a price. Especially love.</span>

<div id="review_2000646617" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2000646617" />
    <a title="Helen 2.0" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39575951-helen-2-0"><img alt="Helen 2.0" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460553725p2/39575951.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2000646617?book_show_action=true">May 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Helen 2.0" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Helen 2.0" href="/user/show/39575951-helen-2-0">Helen 2.0</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=scifi">scifi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=royalty">royalty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2000646617" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8663280918512154166">Oh gosh. It's that time of the month again.<br/><br/><b>Unpopular opinion time</b>, that is!<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1529161027i/25801136.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Queen of All that Dies takes place many years in our future, after one man aggressively took over the entire eastern hemisphere and is on the verge of defeating the Americas in nuclear war. King Lazuli is ruthless and rumored to be immortal. <br/>The main character, Serenity, is an American ambassador sent to Geneva to talk/seduce/coerce the king into granting her nation favorable terms of surrender. She soon discovers that op</span>
  <span id="freeText8663280918512154166" style="display:none">Oh gosh. It's that time of the month again.<br><br><b>Unpopular opinion time</b>, that is!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1529161027i/25801136.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Queen of All that Dies takes place many years in our future, after one man aggressively took over the entire eastern hemisphere and is on the verge of defeating the Americas in nuclear war. King Lazuli is ruthless and rumored to be immortal. <br>The main character, Serenity, is an American ambassador sent to Geneva to talk/seduce/coerce the king into granting her nation favorable terms of surrender. She soon discovers that option #2 is her best bet. This book is primarily a love story between Serenity and King Lazuli. <br><br><u>
  <b>Serenity</b>
</u><br>For a romance main character, Serenity is unique in that she is cast as a villain. <b>A violent, trigger-happy, unreasonable villain</b>. She watched her mother die at 8, killed her first men at 12, joined the army at 15. Because the book is narrated in first person, we get full evidence that Serenity sees herself as a cold-hearted monster. We also get confirmations from her at times brutal actions.<br>However there are traces of <b>irritating YA lead</b> in her, well showcased in a scene where she puts on a dress and makeup: <blockquote>
  <i>I realize for the first time in maybe ever that I'm pretty. It's a shock, and not a pleasant one either. <br>In war, beauty is a curse - it catches your enemies' attention, and you don't want that.</i>
</blockquote> Another annoying trait of Serenity's is her hot-and-cold attitude towards everything. She changes her mind completely, on huge issues like her feelings towards the king and the two nations, in a matter of seconds. I'm not sure if this was due to inconsistent/sloppy characterization by the author, or if Serenity was meant to be a <b>fickle as all hell</b>.<br><br><u>
  <b>King Montes Lazuli</b>
</u><br>The king is an interesting character. He's an objectively awful person on cosmic scales; he's ordered innocent civilians killed, let people starve and die of sickness by the millions when he could have helped, and built himself lavish palaces while his nations' economies crumble. There is no redeeming this man. <br><b>Montes is clearly evil</b>, but that side of him is difficult to catch in QoAtD because he's so busy fawning over Serenity. The book sports a serious case of <b>One-Sided InstaLove</b>. Here's a quote from the first time the king catches sight of Serenity from across the room: <blockquote>
  <i>The world doesn't stop moving, the room doesn't go quiet, but I swear something inside me just broke and reformed the moment she turned her devilish eyes on me - and that's the only way to describe those eyes of hers. Devilish. She's a wicked soul, through and through. <br>Just like me.</i>
</blockquote> So it takes one look for Montes to become borderline obsessed with her. <br>One Sided InstaLove isn't automatically a dealbreaker for me. There are cases where it actually enhances a romantic plotline. For example, when one character experiences love-at-first-sight but the narrative doesn't reveal this fact until after the couple has come together; this way the romantic suspense and the will-they-won't-they excitement is preserved. Jeaniene Frost in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1421990.Halfway_to_the_Grave__Night_Huntress___1_" title="Halfway to the Grave (Night Huntress, #1) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Halfway to the Grave</a> does this fabulously well. <br>However, in QoAtD Montes instantly admits to being enamored with Serenity, which takes all the fun out of the process of falling in love.<br><br><u>
  <b>The Romance</b>
</u> - light spoilers below<br>Finally we arrive at the Central Issue of the book. <blockquote>
  <i>We are the epitome of dysfunction. We are miserable human beings. And yet, when he laces his finger through mine and I feel the thrill of contact, that tiny flame of hope I carry around flares up. <br>Anything's possible. From darkness to light, war to peace - hate to love. <br>We're two monsters who might not be so monstrous after all.</i>
</blockquote><br>I'm a big sucker for <b>enemies to lovers</b> romance stories. From the blurb and the reviews, this seemed like an original twist on that trope. But this plot features a distinct power imbalance between Montes and Serenity, where Montes holds all the cards and Serenity is forced to play for the sake of her people. <br><b>So may I warn all prospective readers: there are several instances of dubious consent, bordering on non-consensual smut in this book.</b><br>Montes is strongly interested in Serenity and her body. Serenity is under an enormous amount of pressure, from her country, her own moral instincts, and Montes himself to give in. It's clear from the dialogue in the book that Montes feels he can do whatever he likes to Serenity, no matter her feelings about it. <br>Within days of meeting her, he corners and tries to kiss her: <blockquote>
  <i>"Are you going to let me kiss you?" the king asks.<br>"Does my answer even matter?" I flick my gaze up to his. <br>"No, not when you're looking at me like that."</i>
</blockquote><br>Here is the happy couple's conversation about Serenity giving Montes her virginity: <blockquote>
  <i>"I'm not a nice man," he says. <br>"I couldn't agree more," I say. <br>"This is happening tonight." <br>My throat works. "I know."<br>"Good."</i>
</blockquote> Serenity later mentions that the thought repulses her. <br>When they finally get down to it, she is still <b><i>clearly</i> unwilling</b>! <blockquote>
  <i>A stray tear streaks down my cheek. "I hate you," I say to him. <br>"You won't always feel that way," he says, thrusting into me. <br>"I will. I swear it."<br>"Give it up," he growls, pushing into me harder.</i>
</blockquote><br>No matter how I look at it, I can't interpret these scenes as romantic. Montes comes off far too rapey to be romantic. It doesn't matter that Serenity eventually falls for the king, or that her "traitorous body" responded to him all along. <b>It's still clear that Montes has no concept of consent</b>, and that doesn't endear him to me as a love interest. <br><br>-<br><br>SOOOO there you have it. I didn't enjoy this book even though most of my friends loved it.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473856615i/20522961._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="8663280918512154166" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1203175022" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1203175022" />
    <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie"><img alt="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505392311p2/11641363.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1203175022?book_show_action=true">Feb 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie">Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24384663-the-queen-of-all-that-dies">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=fantasy-and-magic">fantasy-and-magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=give-this-author-a-bells">give-this-author-a-bells</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1203175022" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3625229745465206709"><b>5 +++ STARS!!!</b><br/><br/>Imagine a future where the world is at war. There is only one ruler. There is no democracy. You either yield to the king or you are his enemy.<br/><br/>Serenity Freeman, is a child of war. All she's ever known is the fight for survival and that her enemy and that of the WUN is King Lazuli, the man responsible for her mother's death and countless others. She's a soldier and it's all she knows, but her father is the emissary of WUN so she's always known that someday she would have to play a pa</span>
  <span id="freeText3625229745465206709" style="display:none"><b>5 +++ STARS!!!</b><br><br>Imagine a future where the world is at war. There is only one ruler. There is no democracy. You either yield to the king or you are his enemy.<br><br>Serenity Freeman, is a child of war. All she's ever known is the fight for survival and that her enemy and that of the WUN is King Lazuli, the man responsible for her mother's death and countless others. She's a soldier and it's all she knows, but her father is the emissary of WUN so she's always known that someday she would have to play a part in forging allegiance.<br><br>First of all the WUN (because you're probably thinking what the heck is that) is the Western United Nations, territory that King Lazuli has not yet conquered. Although it's a wonder that he would like to because it's war torn. After waging war for a decade, the land is riddled with radiation. It's in the water and in the earth. Cancer is the norm for the people who live there. <br><br>Back to the story. Serenity and her father are sent to King Lazuli's territory to begin peace talks. The west is dying, the people are dying and they finally realize that surrender is the only way to move forward. When Montes, King Lazuli sees Serenity, he knows he must have her. And before you roll your eyes no it's not insta-love. You have to understand the type of person Montes is, he has waged wars with the east and west and he always wins. He's a conqueror and he's used to getting his way. And no he's not a alpha jerk, he's ruler of the world and he rules it with an iron fist. He also has a vulnerable side though, because I don't think he quite realised the impact of his actions. The lives he ruined. He never saw the results of his greed until he met Serenity<br><br><b>
  <i>My gaze moves between his eyes, his dark fathomless eyes. "You can't make someone love you," I say.<br>"I don't need you to love me."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402461ra/782291.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424536202i/13774036._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>My Montes minus the beard and the tattoo</i><br><br>Now lets take a moment and give this girl a hand of applause. She's feisty, she's strong and she doesn't take shit from anyone, including King Lazuli. In a nutshell, Serenity Freeman is a kick-ass heroine. I think some might call her abrasive but just remember she's probably the best soldier the WUN has and because of that she's had to deal with men feeling intimidated by her strength. Yes she's attracted to Montes when she first meets him, but she never forgets that he's the man responsible for the death of her beloved Mother.<br><br><b>
  <i>"You want to see compassion? Fine." I take the hand pressed against my shoulders and kiss his knuckles.<br>"I've now kissed the hand of my mother's killer."<br>Before he has time to react to my chaste kiss, I bring my other hand up and slap him.<br>His head whips to the side. "I'm also a vindictive bitch," I say.</i>
</b><br><br>Now did I mention that this is a hate/love romance? A lot of the hate coming from Serenity mind you, but still. Serenity fights her attraction to the king so hard. I think I would too even though he's looks are to die for.<br><br><b>
  <i>The king leans in so that he can peer into my eyes.<br>"Are you alright?"<br>I hold up a finger, and he patiently wait. The nausea passes, and I begin walking again.<br>"What was that?" he asks.<br>"It's my bodies reaction to you."<br>"I'm glad I leave you short of breath."<br>"Don't flatter yourself; I was trying not to barf."</i>
</b><br><br>Now before I bore you anymore than I already have let me say this. The Queen of All That Dies, is thrilling tale filled with suspense, love, hate, passion, lust... and I'm trying to think of more words. It was an awesome read and totally vanquished my book slump only to leave me with yet another one! You should read it! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424536202i/13774037._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>**************************************</b><br><br><b>PRE-REVIEW</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424530124ra/13773224.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I need a moment. This book was fucking awesome!!! But I have a problem... The next book comes out January 2016?!?!?!<br><br>Dear Miss Thalassa<br><br>I suggest you drop all current projects immediately and write The Queen of Traitors. Please.<br><br>Kind Regards<br>A rabid fan.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1564890591" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6522687190711917138"><i>5 devilish stars</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467096965i/19550618.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The world is at war. For <b>Serenity</b> she has known nothing but that, everything has been taken away leaving her with nothing. With her role as the future <i> emissary of the Western United Nations</i>, she must come face to face with the man responsible, the man who is feared above all, the boogey man <b> King Lazuli of the Eastern Empire.</b> She is <i>a pretty lie, a soldier disguised as a lady</i> and the perfect distraction for the King.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re evil and deceptive,” <br/><br/>“And you’re a kindred spir</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText6522687190711917138" style="display:none"><i>5 devilish stars</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467096965i/19550618.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The world is at war. For <b>Serenity</b> she has known nothing but that, everything has been taken away leaving her with nothing. With her role as the future <i> emissary of the Western United Nations</i>, she must come face to face with the man responsible, the man who is feared above all, the boogey man <b> King Lazuli of the Eastern Empire.</b> She is <i>a pretty lie, a soldier disguised as a lady</i> and the perfect distraction for the King.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re evil and deceptive,” <br><br>“And you’re a kindred spirit.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467096965i/19550619._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's scary when you meet the one person you should hate, should despise, but find yourself meeting your match. In her position at the King's side, she threatens the very existence of what the King has stood for. Choosing to fight with her words versus her fists, she weaves compassion into his heart as he shows her the true meaning of absolute power.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He has the same dark soul I do; he knows and embraces my sins, and I’m learning to accept his. I know he is dangerous to be around— dangerous to love— but my heart doesn’t seem to care. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467096965i/19550621._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Realizing she can do more for the people as Queen, she gives her self freely to him. Beneath the anger and the hate, a feeling of desire, of camaraderie, amusement and worse of all...<i>compassion.</i> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We’re the rulers of the entire world; we can do whatever it is we want.”<br><br>“But I still want to punch you in the face.”<br><br>“My queen has never heard of angry sex. I think a woman like you would enjoy it.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467097159ra/19550632.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When the world is turned upside down, and you realize that <i>wrong is right, and right is wrong</i>, you get to know who your true enemy is. A union that was carefully planned, has become stronger than anyone has ever imagined, it puts their lives in danger with only one way to survive. It's a wicked wild road ahead and they have no idea who they are messing with. <br><br><b>The Queen of All that Dies</b> simply put is an amazing read. It was a tale that just pulled me right in, with so much power and so much growth, their story moved me. Serenity is a bad ass, she is one you wouldn't want to piss off, she does what she knows is right using whatever means necessary. The story is told from her point of view, so we become very familiar with her, feeling things as she would and living each moment with her. Through her we get to know the King, he is a mystery to us in the beginning but in the end we understand him on a deeper level. Every man has a weakness and his is Serenity, she makes him be a better man and to see such a man like him give way to her is beautiful. <br><br>One thing I love to see is a strong man fall to his knees, all in the name of love and respect. But it isn't a one way feeling, he softens her around the edges, letting her be who she needs to be and supporting her any way he can. Their relationship is a balance between love and hate, and that in it of itself was enough to keep me glued to the pages, but there is so much more. The added nuances of it being a dystopian novel with a touch of fantasy, it gives us an adventure and mystery with the political alliances. The ending has a WOW factor, one that made me rush out to read the next one, their story is far from over and one would say it really only has just begun. Definitely a recommended read to all my friends who love a robust fanatasical story. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6522687190711917138" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1211202645" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1211202645" />
    <a title="Ivie dan Glokta" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta"><img alt="Ivie dan Glokta" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1441134469p2/9838687.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1211202645?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ivie dan Glokta" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ivie dan Glokta" href="/user/show/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta">Ivie dan Glokta</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=absoute-shaite">absoute-shaite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=bullsh-t">bullsh-t</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=waste-of-time">waste-of-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=horrible-writing">horrible-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=wtf">wtf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=brave-new-world">brave-new-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=i-pity-the-fool">i-pity-the-fool</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=awesome-cover">awesome-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=how-low-can-you-flow">how-low-can-you-flow</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=surprisingly-bad">surprisingly-bad</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1211202645" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4292648826248484464"><b>
  <i>For the first time in my life, I can say I felt embarrassed while reading a book.</i>
</b> <br/><br/>In my time I've read some nonsense, but the sheer ignorance the author displayed in “The Queen of All That Dies” was cringe-worthy to say the least. It came to that point where I couldn't even laugh at it anymore. What made the entire experience bad was all the opportunities the author had but missed to research some points that she chose to incorporate as <u>vital elements</u> of her story. What made it worse is the </span>
  <span id="freeText4292648826248484464" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>For the first time in my life, I can say I felt embarrassed while reading a book.</i>
</b> <br><br>In my time I've read some nonsense, but the sheer ignorance the author displayed in “The Queen of All That Dies” was cringe-worthy to say the least. It came to that point where I couldn't even laugh at it anymore. What made the entire experience bad was all the opportunities the author had but missed to research some points that she chose to incorporate as <u>vital elements</u> of her story. What made it worse is the fact that majority of those were common sense.<br><br>If you ever wondered how to write a cheesy fluffy romance novel, then try to unconvincingly disguise it as politics and intrigue, thus proving you are absolutely clueless about either subject, then by all means, read this book, it will give you some excellent pointers.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424884516ra/13814791.gif" width="500" height="251" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The world has been divided to eastern and western hemispheres by a horrifying nuclear war. Serenity Freeman is living in the burned, barren landscape of the Americas. She lives underground in a kind of military base, with a handful of other survivors. Food is scarce, there is no sunlight. A true post-apocalyptic world. You get the gist of it, now listen to this....<br><br>She is an ambassador's daughter, and in the new world order where every move could mean the difference between life and death , the author chose to apply ancient distribution of power; inheritance, rather than merit as Serenity is called to attend with her father a meeting with the dreaded King Lazuli to negotiate the surrender and survival of an entire hemisphere. I thought OK, maybe she's a badass, highly educated diplomat with mad fighting abilities. The author simply chose to say this, <i>“Next to my father I've learned useful skills.”</i> - what those were, we never discovered. Another thing that stunk to high heaven was the described condition of Canada and Central America. As the author said herself, the things are so unsettled and dangerous there and a ruling government was non existent. Yet, here is this irrelevant girl, <b>
  <i>surrendering</i>
</b> a territory nobody has any control over. It goes so far to say to the reader to disregard her father who happens to have experience as a diplomat, and simply focus on her, because she's speshul and beautiful, and stuff, that on it's own would be enough to dazzle a conquering force...... <br><br><b>
  <u>Seems legit.</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424884331i/13814771.jpg" width="500" height="372" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the midst of all of this <b>
  <i>incredibly clever stuff</i>
</b>, the author launches herself in thinly veiled backhanded praises of just how beautiful Serenity is. She is so malnourished from hunger <i>everybody</i> is suffering from, yet her friend feels sad for her and the look of her hipbones and her collarbones sends them into a grief fest. Never mind that her friend is starving just like she is. Just so we know our MC is super thin guys. The supporting cast keeps subtly hinting how pretty she is, while she selflessly laments her life by having to wear a dress in front of the King, because she is above and beyond superficiality. Oh, and she has a scar, so I guess we were expected to believe she is above vanity as well. To all of those still not getting it, this is the part where the author pretends that <b>by pretending</b> not to like all the frilly, trivial nonsense our MC is actually displaying a sign of incredible depth of character. And, if you wish to continue reading this novel, this is the part where you pretend to believe her.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424884516i/13814792.png" width="396" height="398" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But fuck it, even that isn't bad on it's own. It's the science....<br><br>Most of the developed countries on this planet possess nuclear weapons. Most of the undeveloped countries possess them also. There are a shitload of nukes around, and no matter how turbulent our world becomes, or how violent, nobody ever seems to use them. Why do you think that is? Majority of third-graders out there have an idea. The times of 'Little Boy' are far behind us and most of today's weapons measure in yield up to fifty times more. One single blast from those things and the fallout would encircle the entire Earth in a matter of days. If more then one bombs would detonate we would face a nuclear winter, engulfing the planet in a cloud of smoke that wouldn't lift for decades. Nuclear blasts and radiation are apparently magical in this book. A bomb strong enough to <i>
  <b>level</b>
</i> DC goes off, our heroine survives it in a <i>basement</i>, not a bomb shelter....but a basement. She steps outside after a couple of hours with no ill effects whatsoever, she simply strolls away. <b>
  <i>Many more bombs detonate, across TWO continents covering one half of the globe,</i>
</b> razing the soil, making the atmosphere toxic, and our heroine simply prances around in a dress and heels, waiting for a flight over to Europe. No hazmat suits, no precautions, no Geiger counters, no decon, nothing.<br><br>On top of being magical, the radiation is extremely polite too, as it stayed where it was originally dropped, as Europe continues on with life unscathed, and lush as always. As our Serenity says, the sky is even bluer there... <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424884331i/13814773._SX540_.jpg" alt="you're missing this" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Just think about it... This colossal stupidity is the backstory of the <i>ENTIRE</i> novel. I mean, ignorance on a subject is easily rectified by a little research. If you don't feel confident enough, perhaps don't feature the elements of that subject as carriers for your story. Some time spent with Google at least could save you a shitload of embarrassment. <br><br>Example: <i>Dunning–Kruger effect<br>The Dunning–Kruger effect is a cognitive bias wherein unskilled individuals suffer from illusory superiority, mistakenly assessing their ability to be much higher than is accurate. This bias is attributed to a metacognitive inability of the unskilled to recognize their ineptitude. <br><br>As David Dunning and Justin Kruger of Cornell University conclude: "The miscalibration of the incompetent stems from an error about the self, whereas the miscalibration of the highly competent stems from an error about others."</i><br><br>Did Wikipedia just send you to the <b>BURN UNIT?</b> Oh Yes, I think it did.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430646595ra/14739903.gif" width="304" height="159" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It seemed to me that she was simply too lazy to look anything up, she just tossed all that in there as fluff until she had the chance to focus on the romance. If that is the true case, don't try to sell this novel as something it's not. I simply couldn't go trough this story with a straight face, because the author tried to portray serious characters going trough an incredibly hard life, by saying things that make no goddamn sense at all. Cringe....just cringe..<br><br>PS:<br>Aw hell, i just couldn't keep it in....King Lazuli??? As in Lapis Lazuli??? I kept imagining a smurf. It made those scenes hilarious where she was silently pissed at him. I mean what was she going to do? Choke a smurf? smh... </span>
  <a data-text-id="4292648826248484464" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1260406360?book_show_action=true">Apr 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel E. Carter" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel E. Carter" href="/user/show/29482005-rachel-e-carter">Rachel E. Carter</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1260406360" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2907721897216596756">Agggh, thank you Paige for recommending this book:D<br/><br/>This book is NA and reads like a fast-paced version of Hunger Games meets Shatter Me (not all aspects, obviously, but close!). It definitely has that kind of excitement (and a villainous love interest), and it was addictive as hell. It was also <i>highly</i> quotable. I don't think it'll surprise any of my friends on here that I adore a good love-hate and/or villain-hero relationship and this book was no exception.<br/><br/>Here are a couple of my favorite lines</span>
  <span id="freeText2907721897216596756" style="display:none">Agggh, thank you Paige for recommending this book:D<br /><br />This book is NA and reads like a fast-paced version of Hunger Games meets Shatter Me (not all aspects, obviously, but close!). It definitely has that kind of excitement (and a villainous love interest), and it was addictive as hell. It was also <i>highly</i> quotable. I don't think it'll surprise any of my friends on here that I adore a good love-hate and/or villain-hero relationship and this book was no exception.<br /><br />Here are a couple of my favorite lines:<br /><br /><i>"Time to dance with the devil."<br /><br />"I could have you killed for what you've said to me."<br />"You won't."<br />"Oh, and why is that?"<br />"Because I amuse you."<br /><br />"You're evil and deceptive."<br />"And you're a kindred spirit."</i><br /><br />My only small issues were this:<br />1. The first sex scene <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I did not like that the king went ahead and had sex with Serenity when she still wasn't wanting to. I get that he attracted her and made sure she was turned on first but I just wish he had waited. It felt a little <i>too</i> alpha (which others may enjoy). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />2. Serenity falling in love so quickly. It seemed a bit too quick for me, because her father just died and Lazuli is supposed to be this crazy enemy. Still, it was by no means instalove.<br /><br />And that cliff-hanger??? I love how it is literally leaves everything up in the air. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[You just know Serenity is going to think Lazuli is her enemy again and be brainwashed by the resistance. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1369824490" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1369824490" />
    <a title="Melissa (Ever So Mela)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela"><img alt="Melissa (Ever So Mela)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487543962p2/28640648.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1369824490?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa (Ever So Mela)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa (Ever So Mela)" href="/user/show/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela">Melissa (Ever So Mela)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24384663-the-queen-of-all-that-dies">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Melissa (Ever So Mela) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/9871824-ash">Ash</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela?shelf=na-romance">na-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela?shelf=i-had-high-hopes">i-had-high-hopes</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela?shelf=blur-rating">blur-rating</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1369824490" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6474008306132054586"><b>2.5</b><br/><br/>So, I really won't be able to write a review. As we speak I'm doing this on my cell when I should already be on my way out. <br/><br/>Just going to put a few things out there that irked me...<br/><br/>The age difference honestly creeped me the heck out. The thing is, I never really give it any thought. I mean I constantly read about vampires or some sort of immortal that lives centuries to end up dalling in love with a 20 year old but for some reason, probably because this isn't a paranormal, it creeped the livi</span>
  <span id="freeText6474008306132054586" style="display:none"><b>2.5</b><br /><br />So, I really won't be able to write a review. As we speak I'm doing this on my cell when I should already be on my way out. <br /><br />Just going to put a few things out there that irked me...<br /><br />The age difference honestly creeped me the heck out. The thing is, I never really give it any thought. I mean I constantly read about vampires or some sort of immortal that lives centuries to end up dalling in love with a 20 year old but for some reason, probably because this isn't a paranormal, it creeped the living daylights out of me. At one point I did get over it, but still.<br /><br />The writing... While I can honestly say it was never boring or bogged down on stuff that doesn't matter-interesting even- its read like fanfiction. Now, maybe that's just me, but the actions and monologues felt really amateur. Not that that's bad or anything but it was a slight turn off for me.<br /><br />As for the romance, I don't get it. I got the hate and maybe even the attraction but the reason as to why he must have her or why she fell in love just completely flew over my head. There was no chemistry, at least none that I could see so it ended up falling flat. There was also that one scene where I was just like, <b>NO!!</b> I just wan't comfortable with it.<br /><br />Also, the whole radiation-nuclear-bomb thing? Yeah, how about NO.<br /><br />So in the end, not a bad book but just amazing. I still might read the next book cause the ending wss interesting enough.<br /><br /></span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13610685996879757616"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Mixed Feelings*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote> <br/><b><u>Second re-read</u>:</b> <br/>**<u>CONTAINS SOMEWHAT SPOILERS</u>**<br/>I decided to re-read this book in order to finally get myself to finish this series. Yes, you read that right - I have yet to read the last book. So to make myself catch up with it again, re-reading it seemed like the right choice. The book centers around <b>Serenity Freeman</b> (19), who is the future emissary of the Western United Nations, the last autonomous region of the globe. Meaning she is responsible for forging alli</span>
  <span id="freeText13610685996879757616" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Mixed Feelings*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote> <br><b><u>Second re-read</u>:</b> <br>**<u>CONTAINS SOMEWHAT SPOILERS</u>**<br>I decided to re-read this book in order to finally get myself to finish this series. Yes, you read that right - I have yet to read the last book. So to make myself catch up with it again, re-reading it seemed like the right choice. The book centers around <b>Serenity Freeman</b> (19), who is the future emissary of the Western United Nations, the last autonomous region of the globe. Meaning she is responsible for forging alliances where she can. <b>Now, she's gonna meet the King who killed her mother</b>, and is responsible for millions of lives lost. Expecting to end up in a body body, she's surprised to find that the King can't takes his eyes off of her, and that's when she suddenly understand why she was sent.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“My father killed himself,” the king finally says. “Died at the hand of his own gun. And like you, he was the last family I had.”<br>I stiffen in the king’s arms.<br>“Why are you telling me this?”<br>The king touches my temple. “You have that same look in your eyes he had. It’s been there from the first moment I saw you. And I fear both he and you know a secret I don’t.”<br>I watch the king for a long time, my throat working.<br>“We do.” Never had I imagined my life leading me here, to this moment. Yet now that I’m here, I wonder if there is a beautiful design to things.<br>“Then tell me what it is,” the king says. Those intense eyes are fully focused on me.<br>He doesn’t know; he really has no clue when it’s quite obvious. It’s the secret he continually hides from.<br>“Everything that lives must eventually die.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Overall, while it's still a good read, I got some problems with it</b> that I didn't have before. Like the second we find out the truth about Montes... he kind of looses his edge. Then there the fact that if he's so darn powerful, how come it feels like he got no power when people keep being able to attack him and Serenity? Also the back and forth about how Serenity feels for Montes, <b>got annoying real quick</b>. Though for example the age difference doesn't bother me anymore. That being said, I still enjoyed reading it, but it's definitely going down in rating. Oh and it seems like I have a thing about reading this book in January....<br><br><b><u>Other Characters</u>:</b><br>→ King <b>Montes ‘the Undying King’ Lazuli</b>, of the Eastern Empire. Serenity thinks the king is in his mid thirties. King Lazuli, however, has been conquering countries for nearly thirty years. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Is most likely in his 60's. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b>William ‘Will’ Kline</b>, the general’s son. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Becomes the head of the western chapter of the Resistance at the end of the book. Montes had him killed. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ General <b>Chris Kline</b>, Will’s father. The leader of Serenity's country. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Montes had him killed after Will turned traitor. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ Ambassador <b> Carl Freeman</b>, of the emissary of the Western United Nations (WUN) and Serenity's father. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Carl gets shot and killed by Marco at 38% into the book for refusing to sign the peace treaty in which he would sign Serenity away to Montes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b>Lisa</b>, who owned a wedding dress shop before the war, is now the the residential seamstress since her husband and the rest of her family moved in to the bunkers where Serenity has lived for 5 years.<br>→ <b>Marco</b>, the liaison between Freeman and the king. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[He shoots himself to save the King's secrets at the end of the book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The world we knew is nothing like the one I live in.<br>But none of this, none of it was so costly a price as the one we eventually paid. Somewhere along the way, my people lost the most precious thing of all.<br>Hope.<br>Well, most of us lost it. Most, but not all.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (New Adult) Science Fiction - Dystopia (M/F).<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book One.<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - King Montes Lazuli.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - Umm I don't think so.<br><b>New Rating</b> - 3 stars.<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>Re-read</u>:</b> <br>Ah man, I think, perhaps, that I loved it even more the second time around :O This comes actually as a shock to me. I adore Montes and Serenity is pretty awesome with her ass-kicking ;) Love them! I simply cannot wait for the next book which is only 3 more days away. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><u>First read review</u>:</b><br>NOOOO!! FUCK, HOW CAN YOU END THE BOOK LIKE THAT, LAURA?! I WANT MORE NOW!!!<br>As everyone knows, (if they know me, ofc) I LOVE hate-love relationships, and when I realized that 'The Queen of All that Dies' had that, I was A L L in! + Serenity was a complete kickass heroine :D The book was great, and I cannot wait for the next one. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424716054i/13794880.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>*MIGHT CONTAIN SPOILERS*</b><br>You're probably wondering why I didn't give this a full five stars and the reason is that:<br>1. King Lazuli may have been responsible for killing thousands of people, however he, himself has never ever killed anyone himself.. Though he's all coldblooded and cruel, he lost a bit of that.. how do I say this? Bad boy image, perhaps? I don't know why, but I have a thing for really, and I mean REALLY bad boys... so I was hoping King Lazuli would be a really bad one..<br>2. As King Lazuli and Serenity get more and more close, King Lazuli seem to be getting, softer and losing his...cruelty and his power in a way.. He losing his 'touch'. <br>3. The age difference... 19 and mid-30? Couldn't either he be younger or her be older? <br><br>All in all, this book was awesome and I recommend it to everyone who loves hate-love relationships, war, blood, kickass heroine, alpha male, women who doesn't take crap.. ect..<br><b>Rate</b>: 4 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1882485201" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4140610537831722543"><b> 5 stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “Once upon a time we were innocent, and then we were not.” </i> </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484712112i/21744213._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In the future the world is at war and America is losing the fight against the king. Serenity has only known fighting and horror since she was a kid, and is among the soldiers in the WUN army. Her country is losing the war, and Serenity is sent with her father to make peace agreements with the king. From there it becomes clear she is meant to be an offering to the king, and he likes what he sees.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458616698i/18508485.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> <i> “What you choose to do with </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText4140610537831722543" style="display:none"><b> 5 stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> “Once upon a time we were innocent, and then we were not.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484712112i/21744213._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the future the world is at war and America is losing the fight against the king. Serenity has only known fighting and horror since she was a kid, and is among the soldiers in the WUN army. Her country is losing the war, and Serenity is sent with her father to make peace agreements with the king. From there it becomes clear she is meant to be an offering to the king, and he likes what he sees.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458616698i/18508485.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> <i> “What you choose to do with all that anger is your business. But you can’t control the world; someone will always be there to wrong you. It’s your choice to let it go.” </i> </b><br><br>This is a book I've been meaning to read forever (sorry I took so long Christine) and now finally did. I loved it! An incredibly compelling story, I fell in love with this book right away. It’s just so refreshing to read something different than everything else that’s out there. I had been in a huge book slump before reading this, and this wonderful book pulled me out of it!<br><br>It’s rare when you find a near future dystopian romance that completely sucks you into its world. I felt like I was really there, in the barracks, in the palace. Like a movie playing before my eyes. Giant high five to the author for world building, it’s not an easy feat and she completely nailed it.<br><br>And now I get to the man who makes me and Serenity question our morals and sanity. Montes. The King.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447690196ra/17038191.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But like seriously, I do. Ruthless, cunning, evil. And yet the compassion he showed Serenity, the love he had for her. Damn I wish I could marry this crazy messed up dude LOL.<br><br>Anyways, this book was amazing and unlike anything else I have ever read. If you find yourself intrigued, take the plunge and read this book!<br><br><b> <i> “It should never have been this way. My comrades turning on me, my enemies saving me. But worst of all, I should never have felt anything other than hatred for this man, the king, Definitely not this, this warmth that thaws my soul.<br>I stare into the king's eyes. I am Isolde, I am Juliet, I am Guinevere.<br>I am every one of those idiots because I've fallen for the king.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455783307i/18148833._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4140610537831722543" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3487896471799636682"><b> FUCK FUCK FUCK FUCK FUCK </b><br/><br/>Ever had a good book that makes you wanna slap the people around you because the emotions are just too much?<br/><br/>No?Well, maybe that's just me being violent.Anyway.<br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411741633ra/11269196.gif' width='413' height='240' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>WHAT IS THIS BOOK?!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429593373ra/14610057.gif' width='413' height='226' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Seriously.   <span id="freeText3487896471799636682" style="display:none"><b> FUCK FUCK FUCK FUCK FUCK </b><br><br>Ever had a good book that makes you wanna slap the people around you because the emotions are just too much?<br><br>No?Well, maybe that's just me being violent.Anyway.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411741633ra/11269196.gif" width="413" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>WHAT IS THIS BOOK?!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429593373ra/14610057.gif" width="413" height="226" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously. Why isn't this book more popular?! This book totally rocks! <br><br><b>We have a world in war. A king and an emissary's daughter. She hates him,he loves her. An almost star-crossed love story.</b><br><br><br>The story:<br>The world is at war and the every place in the world is ruined.(This is a dystopian novel, so of course that's given.) Radiation everywhere and food and water is hard to find that people are starving to death.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> There was a time when obesity was the losing battle our people faced. Not so anymore. As soon as food become scarce, curves become coveted.</b>
</blockquote> <br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429593373i/14610058._SX540_.jpg" width="734" height="425" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Serenity Freeman</b> was tasked to face the King for a peace treaty. She practically hates him which is totally understandable seeing he started a war that killed her mom and all the people she cared about.But <b> King Lazuli </b> , bless his heart, has a different opinion for Serenity.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>...and on his arm I see her.<br><br>The emissary's daughter.Serenity Freeman.<br><br>The world doesn't stop moving, the room doesn't go quiet, but I swear something inside me just broke and reformed the moment she turned her devlish eyes on me-and that's the only way to describe those eyes of her.Devlish.She's a wicked soul, through and through.<br><br>Just like me.</b>
</blockquote> <br>See? Totally love it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429593373ra/14610059.gif" width="500" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Thoughts:<br><br>I looove this book. The writing was superb.The characters were perfect and totally no idiotic stunts the H/H pulls. What more can you ask for?<br><br>The King:<br><br>We have a King who was rumored to be undying and who doesn't aged ever since the war started.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>He's even more handsome than the pictures I've seen of him. Black wavy hair, olive skin, dark eyes, sensual lips.But it's more than just his features;it's how he wears them. Like he is something regal, something you want you want to draw closer to.<br><br>It's not fair that evil can wear such an alluring mask.</b>
</blockquote> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429593373i/14610060.jpg" width="236" height="321" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love him. He's the type of character that makes you wonder if he's being a closet good Samaritan or he's just a pure tyrant like what everybody thinks. He loves a good banter with Serenity and he cares for Serenity like a true care-bear.<br><br>And he absolutely knows how to make a girl's heart flutter.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>Finally he speaks. That first moment I saw you," Monte says," I felt a jolt right here," Monte places a hand over his heart" and I knew with a certainty that you were mine."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Serenity:<br><br>A Badass with a capital B. I have a reputation of hating heroines who doesn't do their characters well so color me surprise when I honestly liked Serenity's character. If there's one thing that I loved most about her is that, she doesn't pretend shit.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429593744i/14610138._SY540_.jpg" width="411" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And she's not afraid to speak her mind. In which she fail as a diplomat. Fortunately, that's one of the reason why the she caught the King's attention.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I don't bite." No. I say, "you kill."<br>"So do you, soldier."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>The Romance:<br>We get it that she hates the King at first. But the romance between her and the king is EPIC.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b> I'd never much cared for those epic love stories I'd heard growing up-Romeo and Juliet, Tristan and Isolde, Helen and Paris.All couples who'd placed love above all else; I thought the whole lot of them were idiots.But the way the king is looking at me...now I can see why so many loved those stories.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Yeah yeah. She get's confused at times but you can't blame her for feeling that way. She have known the King as the villain and knowing the real him is bit disorienting.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>We're two monsters who may not be quite so monstrous after all.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>But the scenes. <i> Megahd</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429593373ra/14610062.gif" width="540" height="303" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>I stare into the King's eyes. I am Isolde, I am Juliet, I am Guinevere. I am every one of those idiots because I've fallen for the King.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>But wait a minute.<br><br><b> THE ENDING THE ENDING THE ENDING THE ENDING THE ENDING THE ENDING!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429593373ra/14610063.gif" width="245" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I need a moment..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429593373ra/14610064.gif" width="540" height="303" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br></span>

<div id="review_1200248352" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1200248352" />
    <a title="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin"><img alt="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603831478p2/17438949.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1200248352?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" href="/user/show/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin">Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24384663-the-queen-of-all-that-dies">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin?shelf=fantasy-all">fantasy-all</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin?shelf=kindle-unlimited">kindle-unlimited</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1200248352" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2141232135893474980"><b>UPDATE! THIS IS ON KINDLE UNLIMITED OR $2.99 ON KINDLE. THERE IS ALSO A GIVEAWAY FOR IT ON GR SO DONT MISS OUT ON YHIS AWESOME BOOK! </b> <br/><br/>OMG! I loved this book! It is so full of action, suspense, love, hate, and so much more. <br/><br/>**SPOILERS**<br/><br/>King Lazuli rules the Eastern Empire and he has been waging war with the Western United Nation (WUN) for almost 15 years. Serenity Freeman is on the WUN side of the war and she is a soldier. Her part of the country is dying from starvation, cancer from radiation po</span>
  <span id="freeText2141232135893474980" style="display:none"><b>UPDATE! THIS IS ON KINDLE UNLIMITED OR $2.99 ON KINDLE. THERE IS ALSO A GIVEAWAY FOR IT ON GR SO DONT MISS OUT ON YHIS AWESOME BOOK! </b> <br /><br />OMG! I loved this book! It is so full of action, suspense, love, hate, and so much more. <br /><br />**SPOILERS**<br /><br />King Lazuli rules the Eastern Empire and he has been waging war with the Western United Nation (WUN) for almost 15 years. Serenity Freeman is on the WUN side of the war and she is a soldier. Her part of the country is dying from starvation, cancer from radiation poisoning, not to mention just the war itself. <br /><br />Serenity's father is an emissary for the WUN and she is an apprentice. He taught her from a young age to use and gun and how to fight. She had her first kill at twelve years old when she killed not one, but 4 men who were going to rape her. Sounds like a good kill to me! Her mother was killed when she was younger when the King dropped a bomb near their house. She wants nothing more than to see the King dead. <br /><br />There is something strange about the King, you see pictures of him being shot and seemingly dead but he never is, I wonder what it could be :) <br /><br />The WUN decide to try a peace treaty with the King because they are not going to survive any other way. They send Serenity and her father in as negotiators, they both dread this as none have ever come back alive. They pretty Serenity up in dresses and make up, to her dismay, to try to win the King over. They never in a million years believed it would work, but it does. The King is smitten right away with Serenity, he falls in love with her and can't believe it. She cusses him out at every opportunity, telling him what scum he is and has hit him a few times. This would have resulted in anyone else death but the King can't bring himself to hurt her, he sees a lot of himself in her. <br /><br />Some bad things go down, some really bad things, but she ends up being married to the King and finds herself falling in love with him. She traded herself for her countries life. He gives her all the demands on helping her people that she makes. <br /><br />There is just one big problem, Serenity is dying. Can the King save her with his technology? You have to read to find out. <br /><br />I have to say this book just rocks. It never stops, not once. I could hardly put it down. The way Serenity is so tough and giving the King a run for his money is classic! I love it! <br /><br /><br />THEN ENDING! TALK ABOUT A CLIFFHANGER! I CAN'T WAIT FOR THE SECOND BOOK IN 2016! <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com">www.melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2141232135893474980" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1645938502" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1645938502" />
    <a title="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink"><img alt="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568991289p2/50044222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1645938502?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" href="/user/show/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink">Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=dystopian-scifi">dystopian-scifi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1645938502" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17730898446630314424">Alright. Few things to say right off the bat. I am SUPER conflicted on how to rate this so ignore the stars aspect of this review. <br/><br/>1. As a whole, I definitely enjoyed this series<br/>2. But I have SO many issues with it<br/>3. This is NA not YA.. just incase you guys aren't aware. <br/><br/>So I was kinda confused when I first started this. I couldn't pinpoint the time period- but apparently this is a futuristic / dystopian book. Because of the title, I pinpointed this as fantasy.. so I'm thinking... where's the su</span>
  <span id="freeText17730898446630314424" style="display:none">Alright. Few things to say right off the bat. I am SUPER conflicted on how to rate this so ignore the stars aspect of this review. <br /><br />1. As a whole, I definitely enjoyed this series<br />2. But I have SO many issues with it<br />3. This is NA not YA.. just incase you guys aren't aware. <br /><br />So I was kinda confused when I first started this. I couldn't pinpoint the time period- but apparently this is a futuristic / dystopian book. Because of the title, I pinpointed this as fantasy.. so I'm thinking... where's the suits of armor and the castles? Hah. Okay, there are castles, but they are modern.<br /><br />Anyway, the story overall had a very <b>
  <i>Hades/Persephone vibe</i>
</b> to it. Ready for my no-nonsense and non spoilery summary (well nothing that isn't in the original description)? Here it is: Girl is soldier. Girl is required to go meet the enemy king to try and sway him to make a deal with her country. King meets girl. King is infatuated. King makes a dirty deal. King gets girl. Shit goes down. <br /><br />So I mean- its interesting enough, right? I thought so. Whatever. <br /><br /><u>
  <b>Here is what worked for me:</b>
</u><br /><br />The political intrigue, the planning, and the overall war scenario. Don't get me wrong- it was depressing, but it set the stage. Also, this is completely action packed. After having finished all three books, I can see that Laura carefully planned out the series as a whole instead of writing these books on a whim. Very detailed. The writing was great. The character building was great. <br /><br /><u>
  <b>Here's my issues:</b>
</u><br /><br /><b>The Heroine (Serenity)</b><br /><br />I'm just not Serenity's biggest fan. Maybe we aren't supposed to whole heartedly like (that is the vibe I got from the author anyway) but I just couldn't feel sorry for her. Lets put it this way- she's super messed up and flip flops around about her feelings (which I get) but she's just kinda mean too.<br /><br /><b>Expendable Death</b><br /><br />I was not thrilled about the nonstop expendable death. Serenity apparently knew all her fellow soldiers very well- but she still only referred to them as soldiers -- not by their names or traits or anything. There was TONS of killing, and it felt very brushed over. Also please note that this book is very brutal/graphic.<br /><br /><b>The King (Montez)</b><br /><br />Ugh. I hate this part because I LOVE well developed dark characters. <b>Montez IS very developed and carefully planned out.</b> He was very mysterious, intriguing... I was DYING to know all of his secrets. He's definitely an <b>anti hero</b>... so maybe some of my points are invalid. Whatever, I'm just writing out what I feel. He was completely obsessive, controlling, and forceful on Serenity. The problem I had was not that he was villainous, but that it was kinda romanticized (but also not?) Here's the thing- Serenity constantly admitted that she knew it was messed up but part of her didn't care.. and she was messed up herself. So in a sense, they are both messed up and kinda deserve each other? And I can't say that I didn't enjoy their relationship.. because I did.. but I hated myself for it?? <br /><br /> Welp.. those are my completely incoherent thoughts. Hah. Sorry guys. Take it or leave it.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>Overall</u>
</b><br /><br />I'd say that the series was definitely interesting and enjoyable BUT you have to realize that there are issues with it? <br /><br />And BAM. There's my very non helpful review for a series that I still can't pinpoint and I'll probably remain conflicted. <br /><br /><a href="http://www.herbookishthings.com" rel="nofollow noopener">My Blog</a> ~ <a href="https://www.instagram.com/herbookishthings/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17730898446630314424" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Emer (A Little Haze) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/48320485-zoha">Zoha </a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=challenge-sum2018">challenge-sum2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=trees-died-for-this-crap">trees-died-for-this-crap</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=read2018">read2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=adult-fiction">adult-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=1star">1star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2489434569" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15263983283209546606">No. Ugh. Just no. <br/><br/>This book is awful. It bases itself on an enemies to lovers premise which can very much work... But NOT if you bring in the subject of dubious consent. Let's talk about those words, dubious consent... You know what??? DUBIOUS CONSENT DOES NOT EXIST BECAUSE CONSENT ITSELF IS AN ABSOLUTE!!! It's yes or no. Black or white. Night or day. THERE IS NO GREY IN CONSENT. <br/><br/>UGHHHHHHHHHHHHHH<br/><br/>IT IS NOT FREAKING ROMANTIC TO SAY NO AND THEN HAVE THE MAN DESIRE THE FEMALE MC EVEN MORE AND HAVE H</span>
  <span id="freeText15263983283209546606" style="display:none">No. Ugh. Just no. <br /><br />This book is awful. It bases itself on an enemies to lovers premise which can very much work... But NOT if you bring in the subject of dubious consent. Let's talk about those words, dubious consent... You know what??? DUBIOUS CONSENT DOES NOT EXIST BECAUSE CONSENT ITSELF IS AN ABSOLUTE!!! It's yes or no. Black or white. Night or day. THERE IS NO GREY IN CONSENT. <br /><br />UGHHHHHHHHHHHHHH<br /><br />IT IS NOT FREAKING ROMANTIC TO SAY NO AND THEN HAVE THE MAN DESIRE THE FEMALE MC EVEN MORE AND HAVE HIM FURTHER PURSUE HER AND THEN BASICALLY BLACKMAIL HER INTO MARRIAGE AND A SEXUAL RELATIONSHIP. And then for her to start talking about remorse, angry sex and then have her come to love him because of their twisted Stockholm syndrome-esque relationship!!!! <br /><br />There is no parity in that type of relationship. No matter how much of a badass killer you wanna make this female MC. Her most personal and intimate of relationships started on unequal ground and by the end of this book that had not changed. If sex had been taken out of the equation early on and a more slow burn romance developed then perhaps this may have worked... This was still poorly plotted though with an identikit style cast of characters rather than meaningful portrayals of realistic feeling characters.<br /><br />Look. I get what the author was trying to do but no. She didn't manage it. Instead this book feeds into the rape culture that is so pervasive in society that it somehow romanticises this notion that a woman doesn't know her own mind and when she says no she really means yes but you have to try harder...<br /><br />Ugh <br /><br />No. <br /><br />Sick of this type of BS in books. <br /><br />One star. Would give it less if I could. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br />Read as part of the ABN Summer Reading Challenge recommended by Zoha </span>
